To avoid immediate deadlock and to allow other philosophers a chance to grab a fork, I will grab my left fork first. This is a common strategy in some dining philosophers solutions, as it creates a consistent pattern (e.g., all odd philosophers grab left first, all even grab right first, or everyone grabs left then right). This strategy can lead to a deadlock if not coordinated, but for now, I will take one fork."

If P1 also grabs their left fork, and P3 grabs their left fork, and P4 grabs their left fork, then P5 will be able to grab their right fork. This means P1, P2, P3, P4 have their left fork.
